13  package org.apache.juneau.serializer;
14  
15  import static org.apache.juneau.common.internal.Utils.*;
16  import static org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.*;
17  
18  import java.util.*;
19  
20  import org.apache.juneau.*;
21  import org.apache.juneau.html.*;
22  import org.apache.juneau.json.*;
23  import org.apache.juneau.msgpack.*;
24  import org.apache.juneau.parser.*;
25  import org.apache.juneau.uon.*;
26  import org.apache.juneau.urlencoding.*;
27  import org.apache.juneau.xml.*;
28  import org.junit.jupiter.params.*;
29  import org.junit.jupiter.params.provider.*;
30  
31  /**
32   * Superclass for tests that verify results against all supported content types.
33   */
34  class UriResolution_Test extends SimpleTestBase {
35  
36  	private static class Tester {
37  		final String label;
38  		final Input input;
39  		final Results results;
40  
41  		Tester(String label, Input input, Results results) {
42  			this.label = label;
43  			this.input = input;
44  			this.results = results;
45  		}
46  
47  		void testSerialize(Serializer s, String expected, Object testBean) throws Exception {
48  			try {
49  				var r = s.serializeToString(testBean);
50  
51  				// Specifying "xxx" in the expected results will spit out what we should populate the field with.
52  				if (expected.equals("xxx")) {
53  					System.out.println(label + "/" + s.getClass().getSimpleName() + "=\n" + r.replaceAll("\t", "\\\\t").replaceAll("\\\\", "\\\\\\\\").replaceAll("\\\"", "\\\\\\\"").replaceAll("\n", "\\\\n")); // NOT DEBUG
54  					System.out.println(r);
55  				}
56  
57  				assertEquals(expected, r, fms("{0}/{1} serialize-normal failed", label, s.getClass().getSimpleName()));
58  
59  			} catch (AssertionError e) {
60  				throw e;
61  			} catch (Exception e) {
62  				e.printStackTrace();
63  				throw new AssertionError(label + "/" + s.getClass().getSimpleName() + " failed.  exception=" + e.getLocalizedMessage());
64  			}
65  		}
66  
67  		void testParse(Serializer s, Parser p, Object testBean) throws Exception {
68  			try {
69  				var r = s.serializeToString(testBean);
70  
71  				var m = p.parse(r, TreeMap.class, String.class, String.class);
72  
73  				var r2 = Json5Serializer.DEFAULT.toString(m);
74  				assertEquals(r2, results.json, fms("{0}/{1} parse failed", label, s.getClass().getSimpleName()));
75  
76  			} catch (AssertionError e) {
77  				throw e;
78  			} catch (Exception e) {
79  				e.printStackTrace();
80  				throw new AssertionError(label + "/" + s.getClass().getSimpleName() + " failed.  exception=" + e.getLocalizedMessage());
81  			}
82  		}
83  	}
84  
85  	private static class Input {
86  		final UriContext context;
87  		final UriResolution resolution;
88  		final UriRelativity relativity;
89  
90  		Input(UriResolution resolution, UriRelativity relativity, String authority, String context, String resource, String path) {
91  			this.resolution = resolution;
92  			this.relativity = relativity;
93  			this.context = UriContext.of(authority, context, resource, path);
94  		}
95  	}
96  
97  	private static Input input(UriResolution uriResolution, UriRelativity uriRelativity, String authority, String context, String resource, String path) {
98  		return new Input(uriResolution, uriRelativity, authority, context, resource, path);
99  	}
100 
101 	//------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
102 	// Output
103 	//------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
104 	private static class Results {
105 		final String json, xml, html, uon, urlEncoding, msgPack;
106 
107 		Results(String json, String xml, String html, String uon, String urlEncoding, String msgPack, String rdfXml) {
108 			this.json = json;
109 			this.xml = xml;
110 			this.html = html;
111 			this.uon = uon;
112 			this.urlEncoding = urlEncoding;
113 			this.msgPack = msgPack;
114 		}
115 	}
116 
117 	private static Results results(String json, String xml, String html, String uon, String urlEncoding, String msgPack, String rdfXml) {
118 		return new Results(json, xml, html, uon, urlEncoding, msgPack, rdfXml);
119 	}
120 
121 	private static Tester tester(String label, Input input, Results results) {
122 		return new Tester(label, input, results);
123 	}
124

584 	@ParameterizedTest
585 	@MethodSource("testers")
586 	void a1_jsonSerialize(Tester t) throws Exception {
587 		var s = JsonSerializer.create().json5().uriContext(t.input.context).uriResolution(t.input.resolution).uriRelativity(t.input.relativity).build();
588 		t.testSerialize(s, t.results.json, new TestURI());
589 	}

591 	@ParameterizedTest
592 	@MethodSource("testers")
593 	void a1c_jsonSerialize_usingConfig(Tester t) throws Exception {
594 		var s = JsonSerializer.create().json5().uriContext(t.input.context).uriResolution(t.input.resolution).uriRelativity(t.input.relativity).applyAnnotations(TestURIc.Config.class).build();
595 		t.testSerialize(s, t.results.json, new TestURIc());
596 	}

602 		t.testParse(s, JsonParser.DEFAULT, new TestURI());
